> d_freq / 2 * 0.006)

. // Temperature rise deemed acceptable
. ** Temperature above 1.5 degrees
. gen temp_above = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace temp_above = 0 if temp_rise <= 1.5
(216 real changes made)

. replace temp_above = 1 if temp_rise > 1.5
(61 real changes made)

. lab var temp_above "Temperature rise above 1.5°C deemed acceptable"

. 
. /*
> Very few people suggested temperatures of 2.5°C or higher to be acceptable:
> 2.5°C -> 9
> 3.0°C -> 4
> 3.5°C -> 2
> 4.0°C -> 2
> 4.5°C -> 0
> 5.0°C -> 4
> Therefore, for the illustration Figure 1a all temperature suggestions of 2.5°C or more are summari
> zed under >= 2.5°C
> */
. gen temp_rise2 = temp_rise

. replace temp_rise2 = 2.5 if temp_rise >= 2.5
(12 real changes made)

. tostring temp_rise2, gen(temp_rise3)
temp_rise3 generated as str3

. sort temp_rise

. lab define temp 1 "0" 2 ".5" 3 "1" 4 "1.5", replace

. encode temp_rise3, gen(temp_rise_cropped) lab(temp)

. lab var temp_rise_cropped"All those suggesting 2.5 or more collected in 2.5"

. drop temp_rise2 temp_rise3

. 
.

> Carbon price suggestions tested
> Different models suggest different minimal global carbon prices to stay below a certain temperatur
> e rise. In the main paper we use USD60 as thte threshold. As robustness test, we also test against
>  other specifications: 82 USD, 185 USD, 281 USD
> */
. foreach i in 37 60 82 185 281 {
  2.         gen price_below_`i' = .
  3.                 replace price_below_`i'= 1 if carbon_price < `i'
  4.                 replace price_below_`i'= 0 if carbon_price >=  `i'
  5.         lab var price_below_`i' "Price below USD `i' suggested"
  6. }
(277 missing values generated)
(119 real changes made)
(158 real changes made)
(277 missing values generated)
(151 real changes made)
(126 real changes made)
(277 missing values generated)
(175 real changes made)
(102 real changes made)
(277 missing values generated)

. // Fig. 1c. Marginsplot global carbon price and home carbon price deemed necessary 
. * Set globals
. global info_source info_cc_1 info_cc_2 info_cc_3 info_cc_4 info_cc_5

. global socioeconomics edu1 edu3 edu4 edu5 // Education ref. cat.: edu2 (Social Sciences); gender a
> nd age erased to not jepardize anonimity of participants

. global orga orga2 orga3 orga4 // Governmental organization ref. cat.

. global countryspecifics lower_middle_income upper_middle_income high_income // Income level: ref.c
> at: low

. 
. 
. * Probit, DV: Global carbon price 
. quietly: probit price_below temp_above tech_ms_pca $info_source $orga cops_attended $socioeconomic
> s i.income , vce(robust)

. eststo p1: margins, dydx(tech_ms_pca) post

Average marginal effects                        Number of obs     =        277
Model VCE    : Robust

Expression   : Pr(price_below), predict()
dy/dx w.r.t. : tech_ms_pca

------------------------------------------------------------------------------
             |            Delta-method
             |      dy/dx   Std. Err.      z    P>|z|     [95% Conf. Interval]
-------------+----------------------------------------------------------------
 tech_ms_pca |   .0574945   .0205535     2.80   0.005     .0172105    .0977786
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

. 
. * Probit, DV: Carbon price home now
. quietly: probit price_below_home_now temp_above tech_ms_pca $info_source $orga cops_attended $soci
> oeconomics i.income , vce(robust)

. eststo p2: margins, dydx(tech_ms_pca) post

Average marginal effects                        Number of obs     =        277
Model VCE    : Robust

Expression   : Pr(price_below_home_now), predict()
dy/dx w.r.t. : tech_ms_pca

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

             |      dy/dx   Std. Err.      z    P>|z|     [95% Conf. Interval]
-------------+----------------------------------------------------------------

------------------------------------------------------------------------------

. /*
> Three participants answered the survey twice; same e-mail adress twice in data
> set. For each couple, same name&lastname:
> 
> Date            firstname                               lastname              
>   email
> 04.11.2020      Ram Prasad                              Awasthi               
>   awasthiramprasad@gmail.com
> 16.02.2021      Ram                                             Awasthi       
>           awasthiramprasad@gmail.com
> 
> 02.12.2020      Nagla                                   Jebory                
>   nagla_fnc@yahoo.com
> 05.11.2020      Nagla Mahgoub Hamadain  Jebory                  nagla_fnc@yaho
> o.com
> 
> 06.11.2020      Augustin                                Ngenzirabona    augung
> enzi@yahoo.fr
> 25.03.2021      Ngenzirablna                    Augustin                augung
> enzi@yahoo.fr
> 
> Keep first entry of each
> */

. /*
> Three participants answered the survey twice; same e-mail adress twice in data
> set. For each couple, same name&lastname:
> 
> Date            firstname                               lastname              
>   email
> 04.11.2020      Ram Prasad                              Awasthi               
>   awasthiramprasad@gmail.com
> 16.02.2021      Ram                                             Awasthi       
>           awasthiramprasad@gmail.com
> 
> 02.12.2020      Nagla                                   Jebory                
>   nagla_fnc@yahoo.com
> 05.11.2020      Nagla Mahgoub Hamadain  Jebory                  nagla_fnc@yaho
> o.com
> 
> 06.11.2020      Augustin                                Ngenzirabona    augung
> enzi@yahoo.fr
> 25.03.2021      Ngenzirablna                    Augustin                augung
> enzi@yahoo.fr
> 
> Keep first entry of each
> */
. drop if firstname == "Ram" & lastname == "Awasthi"
(1 observation deleted)

. drop if firstname == "Nagla Mahgoub Hamadain" & lastname == "Jebory"
(1 observation deleted)

(1 observation deleted)

. /* 
> 1: CO2 emissions (metric tons per capita)       
> 2: Droughts, floods, extreme temperatures (% of population, average 1990-2009)
> 3: GDP (constant 2015 US$); 
> 4: GDP growth (annual %)
> 5: GDP per capita (constant 2015 US$)
> 6: Population, total
> */
. 
. drop seriesname 

. encode countryname , gen(country_code)

. reshape wide average , i(country_code) j(indicator)
(note: j = 1 2 3 4 5 6)

Data                               long   ->   wide
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Number of obs.                     1596   ->     266
Number of variables                   4   ->       8
j variable (6 values)         indicator   ->   (dropped)
xij variables:
                                average   ->   average1 average2 ... average6
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

.

.

. label var gdppc "GDP per capita (constant 2015 US$)"

.

. label var population "Population, total"

.

. encode countryname , gen(country_code)

. reshape wide average , i(country_code) j(indicator)
(note: j = 1 2 3 4)

Data                               long   ->   wide
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Number of obs.                      858   ->     216
Number of variables                   4   ->       6
j variable (4 values)         indicator   ->   (dropped)
xij variables:
                                average   ->   average1 average2 ... average4
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

. 
. * Unify variable names
. rename countryname country_home

. label var country_home "Home country"

. drop country_code

. order country_home

. 
. rename average1 control_corr 

. lab var control_corr "Control of Corruption: Estimate [CC.EST]" 

. 
. rename average2 gov_effect

. lab var gov_effect "Government Effectiveness: Estimate [GE.EST]"

.

.

.

> 
> Date            firstname                               lastname              
>   email

>   awasthiramprasad@gmail.com
> 16.02.2021      Ram                                             Awasthi       
>           awasthiramprasad@gmail.com
> 
> 02.12.2020      Nagla                                   Jebory                
>   nagla_fnc@yahoo.com

> o.com
> 
> 06.11.2020      Augustin                                Ngenzirabona    augung
> enzi@yahoo.fr
> 25.03.2021      Ngenzirablna                    Augustin                augung
> enzi@yahoo.fr
> 
> Keep first entry of each
> */

. // World development indices
. *import excel "$xls\WDI_Indexes_average 2015-2019", sheet("Sheet1") firstrow c
> ase(lower) clear
. 
. import excel "$xls\Data_Extract_From_World_Development_Indicators", sheet("Dat
> a") firstrow case(lower) clear
(9 vars, 1,601 obs)

. foreach var in yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019 {
  2. replace `var' = "." if `var' == ".."
  3. }
(325 real changes made)
(333 real changes made)
(333 real changes made)
(336 real changes made)
(581 real changes made)

. destring yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019, replace
yr2015: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(330 missing values generated)
yr2016: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(338 missing values generated)
yr2017: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(338 missing values generated)
yr2018: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(341 missing values generated)
yr2019: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(586 missing values generated)

. encode countrycode, generate(country_code)

. egen average = rowmean(yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019)
(329 missing values generated)

. keep countryname average seriesname

. drop if countryname == ""
(3 observations deleted)

. 
. * Reshape to wide
. egen indicator = group(seriesname)
(2 missing values generated)

. drop if indicator == . // Datasource information
(2 observations deleted)

. 
. /* 
> 1: CO2 emissions (metric tons per capita)       
> 2: Droughts, floods, extreme temperatures (% of population, average 1990-2009)
> 3: GDP (constant 2015 US$); 
> 4: GDP growth (annual %)
> 5: GDP per capita (constant 2015 US$)
> 6: Population, total
> */
. 
. drop seriesname 

. encode countryname , gen(country_code)

. reshape wide average , i(country_code) j(indicator)
(note: j = 1 2 3 4 5 6)

Data                               long   ->   wide
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Number of obs.                     1596   ->     266
Number of variables                   4   ->       8
j variable (6 values)         indicator   ->   (dropped)
xij variables:
                                average   ->   average1 average2 ... average6
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

. 
. * Unify variable names
. rename countryname country_home

. label var country_home "Home country"

. drop country_code

. order country_home

. 
. rename average1 co2_emissionpc

. label var co2_emissionpc "CO2 emissions (metric tons per capita)"

. 
. drop average2 // no values for countries in dataset

. 
. rename average3 gdp

. label var gdp "GDP (constant 2015 US$)"

. 
. rename average4 gdp_growth

. label var gdp_growth "GDP growth (annual %)"

. 
. rename average5 gdppc

. label var gdppc "GDP per capita (constant 2015 US$)"

. 
. rename average6 population

. label var population "Population, total"

. 
. 
.

. * IV) Merge country-specifics

. // World development indices
. *import excel "$xls\WDI_Indexes_average 2015-2019", sheet("Sheet1") firstrow c
> ase(lower) clear
. 
. import excel "$xls\Data_Extract_From_World_Development_Indicators", sheet("Dat
> a") firstrow case(lower) clear
(9 vars, 1,601 obs)

. foreach var in yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019 {
  2. replace `var' = "." if `var' == ".."
  3. }
(325 real changes made)
(333 real changes made)
(333 real changes made)
(336 real changes made)
(581 real changes made)

. destring yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019, replace
yr2015: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(330 missing values generated)
yr2016: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(338 missing values generated)
yr2017: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(338 missing values generated)
yr2018: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(341 missing values generated)
yr2019: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(586 missing values generated)

. encode countrycode, generate(country_code)

. egen average = rowmean(yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019)
(329 missing values generated)

. keep countryname average seriesname

. drop if countryname == ""
(3 observations deleted)

. 
. * Reshape to wide
. egen indicator = group(seriesname)
(2 missing values generated)

. drop if indicator == . // Datasource information
(2 observations deleted)

. 
. /* 
> 1: CO2 emissions (metric tons per capita)       
> 2: Droughts, floods, extreme temperatures (% of population, average 1990-2009)
> 3: GDP (constant 2015 US$); 
> 4: GDP growth (annual %)
> 5: GDP per capita (constant 2015 US$)
> 6: Population, total
> */
. 
. drop seriesname 

. encode countryname , gen(country_code)

. reshape wide average , i(country_code) j(indicator)
(note: j = 1 2 3 4 5 6)

. *ed country_home _merge if _merge == 1
. drop if _merge == 2
(115 observations deleted)

. sum income_level low_income lower_middle_income upper_middle_income high_incom
> e 

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
income_level |        277    2.512635    1.051579          1          4
  low_income |        277    .1805054     .385304          0          1
lower_midd~e |        277    .3718412     .484171          0          1
upper_midd~e |        277    .2021661    .4023423          0          1
 high_income |        277    .2454874    .4311547          0          1

. drop _merge

. 
. * Delegation
. merge m:1 firstname lastname using "$datapath\delegation.dta" // 

    Result                           # of obs.
    -----------------------------------------
    not matched                             1
        from master                         1  (_merge==1)
        from using                          0  (_merge==2)

    matched                               276  (_merge==3)
    -----------------------------------------

. *ed country_home _merge if _merge == 1
. drop if _merge == 2
(0 observations deleted)

. drop _merge

.

>

> 16.02.2021      Ram                                             Awasthi

>

>   nagla_fnc@yahoo.com

> o.com
> 
> 06.11.2020      Augustin                                Ngenzirabona    augung
> enzi@yahoo.fr

> enzi@yahoo.fr

> Keep first entry of each
> */

. *** NDCs and Ratchet Mechanism
. ** Question 1
. foreach var in a1sq001 a1sq002 a1sq003 {
  2. replace `var'="Somewhat better" if `var'=="Somewhatbetter"
  3. }
variable a1sq001 was str14 now str15
(95 real changes made)

(100 real changes made)

(94 real changes made)

.

> mewhat better" 5 "Much better" 99 "Don’t know"
